Comment: dawnherman said "My friends with Crohn's disease will recognize this piece of paper labeled "Low Residual Diet". Sunday is my meal planning day and I usually enjoy it! But this week it involves buying heaps of Gatorade and unhealthy foods to prep for a routine colonoscopy on Friday. Allowed on the low residual diet: white bread, refined cereals, canned fruit. Not allowed: whole wheat bread, whole grain cereal, fresh fruit. Yep, I'm basically not allowed to eat healthy. This is why I started drinking Shakeology four years ago. When I was first diagnosed, most healthy foods aggravated my Crohn's symptoms, so Shakeology was a way to ensure I was getting all the vitamins and nutrients I needed. Since my Crohn's has been in remission I thankfully am able to eat many of those healthy foods now. I'm very grateful for that since I have friends who still have to eat from the unhealthy list."

I strongly believe that everyone HAS time- it's just a matter of what's truly important to them and how bad they want it.
